<div class="post-title">
<h2>Mo Brooks hammers ‘racist’ $5 billion carve-out for minority farmers in COVID ‘stimulus’ at Dothan campaign stop — ‘This is insulting’</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Brooks-1.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(Jeff Poor/YHN)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>DOTHAN — Fresh off his announcement of a run for U.S. Senate days earlier, U.S. Rep. Mo Brooks (R-Huntsville) made a stop in the southeastern corner of the state on Thursday to woo GOP voters more than a year ahead of the 2022 Republican primary.</p>
<p>In his 2017 bid for U.S. Senate, Brooks <a href="https://www.nytimes.com/elections/results/alabama-senate-special-election-primary">struggled in the Wiregrass region</a>, finishing a distant third to then-U.S. Sen. Luther Strange (R-Mountain Brook) and former Alabama Supreme Court chief justice Roy Moore, who was the eventual Republican nominee. Brooks is seeking to change that in next year’s Republican U.S. Senate primary and started early with an appearance at the Houston County Republican Women’s monthly luncheon.</p>
<p>During his speech, Brooks defended his decision to challenge the outcome of the 2020 presidential election and also discussed the consequences of Democrat control of the federal government. Among those, he addressed the nearly $2 trillion COVID-19 relief package passed earlier this month, which included $5 billion for <a href="https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2021/03/08/reparations-black-farmers-stimulus/">“farmers of color.”</a></p>
<p>Brooks slammed Democrats’ decision to include that provision in the coronavirus package, deeming it “insulting” and “racist.”</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            395</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">395 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/mo-brooks-hammers-racist-5-billion-carve-out-for-minority-farmers-in-covid-stimulus-at-dothan-campaign-stop-this-is-insulting/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">395 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>“There’s something really bad in this bill — their $2 trillion borrow-and-spend bill passed a couple of weeks ago,” he said. “How many of y’all are familiar with the $5 billion that has been set aside for farmers? Raise your hand if you’ve heard of it. A few of you have. This is insulting. It is racist to the worst degree because you know which farmers have access to it? All of them except for whites. If you’re a Native American farmer, you get a slice of that $5 billion. If you’re an Asian-American farmer, you get a slice of that $5 billion. If you’re a Spanish-American farmer, you get a slice of that $5 billion. If you’re an African-American farmer, you get a slice of that $5 billion. But if you happened to have been born with a white complexion — if you’re Caucasian, forget it. You’re out. Whites need not apply.”</p>
<p>“Now, racism is wrong everywhere, OK?” Brooks added. “We fought a Civil War about it, where hundreds of thousands of people lost their lives in large part because of that issue. There were other issues, but that was a big part of it. And the 14th Amendment says equal protection. But these socialists, who exploit and create racial division for political gain — they’re doing this for political gain. They’re seeking bloc votes based solely on skin pigmentation. And I would submit to you that is repulsive and that is wrong. It was wrong when African-Americans were discriminated against. It is wrong if Asian-Americans are discriminated against. It is wrong if Native Americans are discriminated against. It wrong with respect to any kind — we’re all Americans. And we need to be skin color-blind because skin pigmentation is an accident of birth. But that’s not the way it is on the socialist side of the coin. They want to magnify it, and they want to exploit it. They want to divide us rather than bring us together. That is horrible, and we should never let them get away with it.”</p>
<p>Brooks told the audience the key to stopping those efforts was getting involved in elections.</p>
<p><strong><em><a href="http://twitter.com/jeff_poor">@Jeff_Poor</a> is a graduate of Auburn University and the University of South Alabama, the editor of <a href="https://www.breitbart.com/clips">Breitbart TV</a>, a columnist for Mobile’s <a href="https://lagniappemobile.com/category/commentary/beltway/">Lagniappe Weekly</a>, and host of Mobile’s “The Jeff Poor Show” from 9 a.m.-12 p.m. <a href="http://www.fmtalk1065.com/">on FM Talk 106.5</a>.</em></strong></p>
</p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Huntsville-based HomeTown Lenders seeking to raise $1 million for St. Jude this year</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/HomeTown-Lenders-St-Jude.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(HomeTown Lenders/Facebook, YHN)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p><a href="https://htlenders.com">HomeTown Lenders (HTL)</a> on Thursday announced a major partnership with St. Jude Children’s Research Hospital that will strive to generate $1 million this year to support the hospital’s mission of finding cures and ultimately saving children’s lives.</p>
<p>In a press release, HTL outlined that it has set a goal of donating at least $1 million to St. Jude in 2021 alone. Many of HTL’s ninety-one branches across the country will participate in the ambitious effort.</p>
<p>Participating branches this year will donate a minimum of $50 for every loan closed to the hospital, where no family receives a bill for treatment, travel, housing or food – because all a family should worry about is helping their child live.</p>
<p>HTL, which is headquartered in Huntsville and has six additional <a href="https://htlenders.com/branches/locations/AL">branches</a> around the Yellowhammer State, views the new St. Jude partnership as an avenue to serve others while implementing the company motto: “People Over Profits.”</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            201</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">201 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/huntsville-based-hometown-lenders-seeking-to-raise-1-million-for-st-jude-this-year/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">201 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>“Our customers and staff always jump at a challenge, and we have intentionally set a bold goal – one that underscores our motto, People over Profits,” stated Billy Taylor, CEO of HomeTown Lenders.</p>
<p>“Throughout 2021, we will strive to raise our community outreach standard and give back to the local communities in which we live and work by donating hard-earned revenue to a tremendously worthwhile cause,” he continued. “Childhood cancer is a disease that affects so many, and we are eager to join the fight to end it. The St. Jude team in Memphis does a remarkable job of researching effective treatments and potential cures for our most valuable resources: our young people. I could not be prouder of our team for taking the bull by the horns and raising the bar this year.”</p>
<p>As the only National Cancer Institute-designated Comprehensive Cancer Center devoted solely to children, treatments invented at St. Jude have helped push the overall childhood cancer survival rate from 20% to 80% since the hospital opened more than 50 years ago. And St. Jude has pledged not to stop until no child dies from cancer.</p>
<p><em>Sean Ross is the editor of Yellowhammer News. You can follow him on Twitter <a href="https://twitter.com/sean_yhn">@sean_yhn</a></em></p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Five deaths confirmed so far as reports of tornadoes, storms, flash floods pour in from across Central and North Alabama</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Alabama-Storms-Lightning-Weather.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(YHN/Pixabay)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>Five people are confirmed dead in the Calhoun County town of Ohatchee as Alabama undergoes an enormous bout of severe weather, including tornadoes that have touched down in various locations from the Black Belt across the Birmingham area and into Northern Alabama.</p>
<p>The Calhoun County Emergency Management Agency published a release at 4:26 p.m. confirming “multiple reports of injuries and fatalities.”</p>
<p>A number of reporters from television stations in Birmingham have reported that the current number of <a href="https://twitter.com/stephenq3340/status/1375213484854624256?s=21">confirmed</a> casualties is five.</p>
<p>Dangerous storms remain active in several locations in Alabama as of 4:43 p.m. Citizens are encouraged to turn on local radio stations and TV channels for up to the minute coverage.</p>
<p>If encountering downed power lines or dangerous debris, members of the public are encouraged to turn around let authorities deal with the situation.</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            224</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">224 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/five-deaths-confirmed-so-far-as-reports-of-tornadoes-storms-flash-floods-pour-in-from-across-central-and-north-alabama/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">224 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>Ohatchee, currently the only town with confirmed fatalities from the weather, is a small town of around 1,100 people located northwest of Anniston.</p>
<p>Significant tornado damage has been reported in a number of Shelby County cities as a result of an as yet uncounted number of tornadoes.</p>
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet" data-dnt="true" data-width="500">
<p dir="ltr" lang="en">A family reunification location has been established in the parking lot of Baumhower's at 1001 Doug Baker BLVD STE 112, Birmingham, AL 35242 for the Eagle Point Subdivision. If you need assistance in locating family members from this area, please speak with law enforcement here.</p>
<p>— Shelby County SO (@ShelbyCountySO) <a href="https://twitter.com/ShelbyCountySO/status/1375184036172328968?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">March 25, 2021</a></p></blockquote>
<p><script async="" charset="utf-8" data-rocketlazyloadscript="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"></script></p>
<p>Road-closing levels of floods have been reported from areas around Birmingham up through Alabama’s border with Tennessee.</p>
<p>Authorities are urging citizens “Turn around, don’t drown,” when they see water over the roads.</p>
<p>A police officer in Florence was struck by lightning during the storms but is now <a href="https://twitter.com/HDrinkardTV/status/1375191111896031245">reportedly</a> “awake and alert.”</p>

<p>The State of Alabama’s extreme weather preparedness resources <a href="https://ema.alabama.gov/preparedness/">can be found here</a>.</p>
<p>“Significant and dangerous weather continues to impact portions of Alabama, and I urge all folks in the path of these tornadoes and storm systems to remain on high alert. Tragically, we are receiving reports of loss of life,” said Governor Kay Ivey in a statement shortly after 5:00 p.m. on Thursday.</p>
<p>“I offer my sincerest prayers to all impacted. Unfortunately, the day is not over yet. Y’all, please stay safe and vigilant!” the governor exhorted.</p>
<p><strong>UPDATE 5:34 p.m.</strong></p>
<p>This draft was updated to reflect the casualty count in Ohatchee increasing from three to five.</p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Amazon exec: While Bernie Sanders talks about a $15 minimum wage, we actually provide it — ‘Should save his finger wagging lecture until after he actually delivers’</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Bernie-Sanders-2.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(Gage Skidmore/Flickr)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>U.S. Senator Bernie Sanders (I-VT) is being called out for not walking the walk ahead of <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/bernie-sanders-to-visit-bessemer-on-friday-as-democrats-hollywood-activists-continue-to-attack-alabamas-right-to-work-status/">his Friday visit</a> to speak with Amazon workers in Bessemer, Alabama.</p>
<p>Sanders is slated to be joined by rapper “Killer Mike” and Hollywood’s Danny Glover on his trip, which will come the same day that first lady Jill Biden and actress Jennifer Garner <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/whats-in-your-wallet-hollywoods-jennifer-garner-to-join-jill-biden-in-alabama-on-friday/">also visit the state. </a></p>
<p>Ahead of Sanders leaving Washington, D.C. to touch down on an Alabama tarmac, one Amazon executive is pointing out some key facts regarding the Democratic socialist former presidential candidate.</p>
<p>Dave Clark, an alumnus of Auburn University and CEO of Amazon’s worldwide consumer business, <a href="https://twitter.com/davehclark/status/1374853182484963332?s=20">took to Twitter</a> this week to underscore that while Sanders spends a lot of time delivering political speeches regarding his support for a $15 minimum wage and health care coverage, Amazon actually delivers both of these items already for its employees.</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            468</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">468 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/amazon-exec-while-bernie-sanders-talks-about-a-15-minimum-wage-we-actually-provide-it-should-save-his-finger-wagging-lecture-until-after-he-actually-delivers/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">468 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>Clark stated that he welcomes Sanders to the Birmingham area and appreciates “his push for a progressive workplace.”</p>
<p>“I often say we are the Bernie Sanders of employers, but that’s not quite right because we actually deliver a progressive workplace,” Clark continued.</p>
<p>He then highlighted that on top of Amazon’s $15 minimum wage, the company <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/amazon-to-hire-1500-full-time-positions-at-bessemer-fulfillment-center/">offers</a> industry-leading benefits to full-time employees, which include comprehensive health care from day one, 401(k) with 50% match, up to 20 weeks paid parental leave and Amazon’s innovative Career Choice program, which pre-pays 95% of tuition for courses in high-demand fields. Since the program’s launch four years ago, more than 25,000 employees have pursued degrees in game design and visual communications, nursing, IT programming and radiology, just to name a few. Clark also underscored Amazon’s “safe and inclusive work environment.”</p>
<p>“So if you want to hear about $15 an hour and health care, Senator Sanders will be speaking downtown. But if you would like to make at least $15 an hour and have good health care, Amazon is hiring,” Clark said.</p>
<p>He subsequently pointed out that Sanders’ home state of Vermont, in which the senator has been a prominent elected official for decades, the minimum wage is well below Amazon’s companywide minimum wage.</p>
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet">
<p dir="ltr" lang="en">All we want to know is why the Sen is one of the most powerful pols in VT for 30+ yrs and their min wage is STILL only $11.75.AMZN’s min wage is $15 + great health care from Day 1.The Sen should save his finger wagging lecture until after he actually delivers in his own backyard. <a href="https://t.co/dRo2Tv1xDQ">https://t.co/dRo2Tv1xDQ</a></p>
<p>— Dave Clark (@davehclark) <a href="https://twitter.com/davehclark/status/1375045409542823939?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">March 25, 2021</a></p></blockquote>
<p><script async="" charset="utf-8" data-rocketlazyloadscript="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"></script></p>
<p>Clark was scheduled to deliver a spring commencement keynote address at Auburn last year before COVID-19 ended those plans. In a March 2020 <a href="https://ocm.auburn.edu/newsroom/news_articles/2020/03/020826-may-commencement.php">release,</a> the university hailed him as a “[s]trategic and visionary” leader with “a commitment to fostering dynamic and innovative work cultures known for employee development and customer satisfaction.”</p>
<p>Sanders’ Friday visit will come as the Bessemer unionization vote winds down. Amazon employees are voting on whether to join the New York City-based Retail, Wholesale and Department Store Union (RWDSU).</p>
<p>Per the <a href="http://www2.labor.alabama.gov/LAUS/LAUScities.pdf">latest available data</a> from the Alabama Department of Labor, Bessemer has the third-highest rate of unemployment among the state’s major cities.</p>
<p>While Sanders is known for railing against the 1%, his net worth is <a href="https://www.celebritynetworth.com/richest-politicians/democrats/bernie-sanders-net-worth/">estimated</a> to be about $3 million. The senator and his wife raked in almost $5 million from 2009-2018. They own three homes. Sanders has not worked in the private sector since 1981 and is currently drawing two separate government pensions.</p>
<p>The likes of <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/tuberville-on-bessemer-amazon-union-vote-president-biden-should-not-have-stepped-in-trying-to-tip-the-scales/">President Joe Biden,</a> U.S. Representative Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez (D-NY) and Georgia Democrat <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/stacey-abrams-joins-aoc-bernie-sanders-in-backing-amazon-unionization-push-in-alabama/">Stacey Abrams</a> have also publicly backed the Alabama unionization effort.</p>
<p><em>Sean Ross is the editor of Yellowhammer News. You can follow him on Twitter <a href="https://twitter.com/sean_yhn">@sean_yhn</a></em></p>
</p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Local students can apply to join The World Games 2022 Birmingham youth choir, perform at opening and closing ceremonies</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/World-Games-2022-Youth-Choir.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(TWG 2022, YHN)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p><a href="https://twg2022.com">The World Games 2022</a> is looking for talented young singers from the Birmingham metropolitan area.</p>
<p>A multi-sport event that will take place in the Magic City from July 7- 17, 2022, The World Games 2022 will see an anticipated 3,600 athletes from over 100 countries participate in more than 30 different sports.</p>
<p>Birmingham’s under-construction Protective Stadium will host the opening and closing ceremonies, at which The World Games 2022 Youth Choir will perform.</p>
<p>It was announced on Thursday that this choir will be comprised of selected local 7th-12th graders.</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            243</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">243 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/local-students-can-apply-to-join-the-world-games-2022-birmingham-youth-choir-perform-at-opening-and-closing-ceremonies/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">243 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>According to a release, a select group of the students will also have the chance to record the official theme song of The Games, composed by Dr. Henry Panion III (the World Games 2022 artistic director) and Randy Owen of the group Alabama.</p>
<p>Applications for the choir will close on April 30, 2021. Those selected to participate will be notified in May. Students can apply <a href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSciY6LMtZN2oLIcNXrMejb6qxbmduoagoSIhNCc0wXBTjoVWQ/viewform?vc=0&amp;c=0&amp;w=1&amp;flr=0&amp;gxids=7628">here.</a></p>
<p>“The opportunity to engage our youth in this historical event is so exciting. They will be part of the memories we all hold and treasure long after the Games are over,” stated The World Games 2022 vice president of community engagement Kathy Boswell.</p>
<p>Rashada LeRoy, president and CEO of LRY Media Group and executive producer of the opening and closing ceremonies, said she is excited to see all the talented young singers from the community who decide to audition.</p>
<p>“What makes Birmingham the ‘Magic City’ is the community,” LeRoy remarked. “There are so many talented and dynamic youth who make our community strong and deserve to have their voices heard for the entire World to see.”</p>
<p>With fans traveling from worldwide destinations to Birmingham and experiencing over 25 unique venues around the greater metropolitan area, <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/the-world-games-is-an-even-bigger-deal-than-you-think-2/">The World Games 2022</a> will generate an estimated $256 million in economic impact.</p>
<p><strong>RELATED: <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/the-world-games-2022-announces-three-of-the-birmingham-venues-to-be-showcased-across-the-planet/">The World Games 2022 announces three of the Birmingham venues to be showcased across the planet</a></strong></p>
<p><em>Sean Ross is the editor of Yellowhammer News. You can follow him on Twitter <a href="https://twitter.com/sean_yhn">@sean_yhn</a></em></p>
</p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Mike Pence headlining Faulkner University benefit dinner in Montgomery this October</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Mike-Pence-Faulkner-University.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(GPA Photo Archive/Flickr, YHN)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>Former Vice President Mike Pence will travel to Montgomery on October 7 to speak at Faulkner University’s annual benefit dinner.</p>
<p>Mike Williams, president of Faulkner University, announced the news Pence was the 2021 speaker at a <a href="https://www.facebook.com/watch/live/?v=773836859906086&amp;ref=watch_permalink">press conference</a> on Thursday morning.</p>
<p>“Mike Pence is a man of deep Christian faith,” said Williams at the unveiling. “He’s been an ardent advocate for liberty, and most expressly religious liberty, the guiding force of our founding fathers who forged this republic.”</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            163</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">163 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/mike-pence-headlining-faulkner-university-benefit-dinner-in-montgomery-this-october/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">163 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>“It is on this foundation of religious liberty that Faulkner stands today,” Williams added.</p>
<p>Previous to his selection as then-candidate Donald Trump’s running mate in 2016, Pence was governor of Indiana and before that a member of the U.S. House of Representatives.</p>
<p>Faulkner’s annual dinners date back more than four decades and have in recent years attracted very prominent names from the world of politics.</p>
<p>Former Trump administration U.N. Ambassador Nikki Haley spoke in 2019, and high-profile former Congressman Trey Gowdy (R-SC) spoke in 2020.</p>
<p>Over the last decade, around 2,000 guests have attended the dinners annually. The event in recent years has been held at the Renaissance Hotel in downtown Montgomery.</p>
<p>A general admission ticket to the 2021 event is $150.</p>
<p>Sponsorship packages are available starting at $2,500 and going up to $40,000 that include photos with and special access to Pence.</p>
<p>Tickets and sponsorships can be <a href="https://www.faulkner.edu/events/2020-benefit-dinner-featuring-mike-pence/">purchased here</a>.</p>
<p><em>Henry Thornton is a staff writer for Yellowhammer News. You can contact him by email: henry@yellowhammernews.com or on Twitter <a href="https://twitter.com/HenryThornton95">@HenryThornton95.</a></em></p>
</p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Shelby: Democrats attempting ‘blatant power grab in an effort to force a federalized election system’</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/10/Richard-Shelby-1.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">Sen. Richard Shelby (R-Ala.)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>U.S. Senator Richard Shelby (R-AL) has come out in firm opposition to S.1, which is Senate Democrats’ version of <a href="https://www.congress.gov/bill/117th-congress/house-bill/1/text">H.R. 1.</a></p>
<p>The legislation, <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/tuberville-democrats-h-r-1-trying-to-make-worst-practices-of-pandemic-era-elections-mandatory-in-all-50-states/">the so-called</a> “For the People Act,” has been <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/mo-brooks-stopping-h-r-1-amnesty-keys-to-winning-in-2022-midterms-then-we-will-be-able-to-neuter-joe-biden/">widely criticized</a> by Republicans. The House recently <a href="https://clerk.house.gov/Votes/202162">passed</a> H.R. 1 without any GOP votes and with bipartisan opposition; U.S. Senator Joe Manchin (D-WV) this week said he would not support the measure unless it received bipartisan support.</p>
<p>On Wednesday, the Senate Rules Committee — of which Shelby is a member and former chairman — <a href="https://www.rules.senate.gov/hearings/s1-the-for-the-people-act">held a hearing</a> on S.1. While Alabama’s senior senator was unable to attend the meeting, Yellowhammer State native and Senate Minority Leader Mitch McConnell (R-KY) was present and asked questions.</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            172</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">172 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/shelby-democrats-attempting-blatant-power-grab-in-an-effort-to-force-a-federalized-election-system/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">172 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<blockquote class="twitter-tweet">
<p dir="ltr" lang="en">Democrats’ H.R. 1 would leave elections more vulnerable to cheating, send taxpayer dollars to subsidize campaigns, and would turn the bipartisan Federal Election Commission into a Democrat-controlled partisan body.</p>
<p>It’s not about protecting voting. It’s about rigging the system. <a href="https://t.co/POrUh2bq9H">pic.twitter.com/POrUh2bq9H</a></p>
<p>— Leader McConnell (@LeaderMcConnell) <a href="https://twitter.com/LeaderMcConnell/status/1374737219165040644?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">March 24, 2021</a></p></blockquote>
<p><script async="" charset="utf-8" data-rocketlazyloadscript="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"></script></p>
<p>On Thursday, Shelby released a statement bashing the legislation as “a blatant power grab in an effort to force a federalized election system on the entire country.”</p>
<p>“Not only would S.1 give unelected, ultraliberal Washington bureaucrats the ability to control how Alabama conducts its elections, but it would open doors to fraud and have a devastating impact on our freedom of speech,” he continued. “Further, S.1 would allow the use of taxpayer dollars for political campaigns. I vehemently oppose this bill and urge every one of my colleagues in Congress to do the same. This legislation would have dangerous implications on the future of our democracy.”</p>
<p><em>Sean Ross is the editor of Yellowhammer News. You can follow him on Twitter <a href="https://twitter.com/sean_yhn">@sean_yhn</a></em></p>
</p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Sessions to keynote Southern Prep’s inaugural scholarship banquet</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Jeff-Sessions-Southern-Prep.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(Jeff Sessions, The Southern Prep Academy/Facebook, YHN)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>Former U.S. Attorney General Jeff Sessions will be the keynote speaker at Southern Preparatory Academy’s first-ever Board of Trustees Scholarship Banquet.</p>
<p><a href="https://southernprepacademy.org/">Southern Prep</a> was known for years as Lyman Ward Military Academy before rebranding in 2019. A boarding school, it bills itself as “Alabama’s premier military academy for boys” and takes young men in grades 6-12.</p>
<p>The banquet at which Sessions will speak is designed to raise money for scholarships to the school, where enrollees are referred to as “cadets.”</p>
<p>“These scholarships can make all the difference in a cadet’s life. They enable promising cadets to pursue a quality education and experience opportunities that otherwise would not have been available,” said Southern Prep in a release.</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            180</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">180 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/sessions-to-keynote-southern-preps-inaugural-scholarship-banquet/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">180 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>The banquet marks a relatively rare public appearance for Sessions, who has kept a low profile after placing second in the 2020 Republican primary to reclaim the U.S. Senate seat he held from 1997-2017.</p>
<p>Southern Prep’s banquet is being held at the Auburn Marriott Opelika Resort and Spa at Grand National. Southern Prep has several rooms blocked off for guests interested in the banquet who want to stay overnight.</p>
<p>According to Southern Prep, the inaugural Board of Trustees Scholarship Banquet is designed ” to bring together cadets, alumni, faculty, families, and friends of the academy for a night of sharing experiences, stories, and a wonderful evening.”</p>
<p>Those interested in attending can purchase an individual registration for $125 or buy a table sponsorship, eight seats in total, for $1,000.</p>
<p>All proceeds go toward scholarships for cadets at Southern Prep.</p>
<p>The page to buy an individual registration or table sponsorship is <a href="https://secure.givelively.org/donate/lyman-ward-military-academy-the-southern-industrial-institute/southern-prep-s-board-of-trustees-banquet">available here</a>.</p>
<p>Those paying, and their guests, need to also fill out a form <a href="https://us4.list-manage.com/survey?u=062309e9cc9d958e1437a2cee&amp;id=e6ac32fb57&amp;attribution=false&amp;e=5e0261f3b5">available here</a>.</p>
<p><em>Henry Thornton is a staff writer for Yellowhammer News. You can contact him by email: henry@yellowhammernews.com or on Twitter <a href="https://twitter.com/HenryThornton95">@HenryThornton95.</a></em></p>
</p>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>Tuberville introduces bill to bar illegal aliens from receiving ‘free pass’ into the United States</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Tommy-Tuberville-fireplace-flag.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(Senator Tommy Tuberville/YouTube)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>U.S. Senator Tommy Tuberville (R-AL) on Thursday introduced a bill that would prohibit detained illegal aliens from being freely released into the United States without at least receiving a court date.</p>
<p>Due to the surge of migrants at the southwest border and overcrowding at detention facilities, U.S. Customs and Border Protection has started to release migrants, who have illegally entered the country before claiming asylum, without issuing a Notice to Appear (NTA) in immigration court for a hearing. An NTA provides illegal migrants with a date and time certain to appear before an immigration judge and plead their case for asylum.</p>
<p>Tuberville’s legislation would require the Department of Homeland Security (DHS) to issue an NTA for removal proceedings to any migrant who has illegally entered the U.S. prior to releasing them into the country or granting parole.</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            335</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">335 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/tuberville-introduces-bill-to-bar-illegal-aliens-from-receiving-free-pass-into-the-united-states/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">335 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-large full_body">
<p>
<p>A release from Tuberville’s office underscored that releasing illegal migrants from detention without an NTA runs counter to the spirit and letter of the law and erodes the integrity of America’s immigration system. By not providing an NTA, the government loses control over who is being released into the United States and deprives migrants of the opportunity to make legitimate asylum claims before an immigration judge.</p>
<p>The bill further stipulates that a migrant’s parole, deferred action or any other immigration status and associated employment authorization will be terminated if they fail to appear for the subsequent hearing after receiving an NTA.</p>
<p>Senators Ted Crux (R-TX), Mike Lee (R-UT), Kevin Cramer (R-ND), Mike Braun (R-IN) and John Barrasso (R-WY) are original cosponsors of Tuberville’s bill.</p>
<p>“Our facilities at the border are bursting at the seams, and because we’ve simply run out of space, we’re releasing illegal migrants into our country with no real accountability, or date to appear in court,” stated Alabama’s junior senator. “At best, it hurts those who come to this country actually looking to plead their asylum case. At worst, it’s giving free rein into our country for breaking the law.”</p>
<p>“This bill would prohibit migrants who came into the country illegally from being released into communities without a notice to appear in immigration court,” Tuberville concluded. “The Biden administration says they want ‘humane’ and ‘compassionate’ improvements to our immigration system – releasing someone without an NTA is neither. President Biden dismantled the successful policies President Trump put in place, but this bill will help restore integrity in our immigration system.”</p>
<p><iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="315" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/EKyseHNfesk" title="YouTube video player" width="560"></iframe></p>
<p>This comes as Tuberville on Thursday and Friday joins Senators John Cornyn (R-TX) and Cruz, and other Republican Senators, on a trip to the southern border. The delegation is visiting McAllen, TX, to speak with CBP officers and see firsthand the processing facilities and ports of entry.</p>
<p><strong>RELATED: <a href="https://yellowhammernews.com/tuberville-cosponsors-stopping-border-surges-act-prevents-the-exploitation-of-our-immigration-laws/">Tuberville cosponsors Stopping Border Surges Act</a></strong></p>
<p><em>Sean Ross is the editor of Yellowhammer News. You can follow him on Twitter <a href="https://twitter.com/sean_yhn">@sean_yhn</a></em></p>
</p>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-less1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-up"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Show less</span>
</a>
</div>

<div class="post-title">
<h2>UPDATE: Ivey issues state of emergency for 46 counties ahead of Thursday’s predicted severe weather</h2>
</div>
<div class="post-image" style="background-image: url('https://yellowhammernews.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/10/Ivey-hurricane.jpg');"></div>
<span class="caption">(Henry Thornton/YHN)</span>
<div class="post-content" data-ids="">
<div class="text-small brief_body test1 test19">
<p>Governor Kay Ivey has issued a state of emergency for 28 counties in Alabama ahead of severe weather anticipated for Thursday.</p>
<p>The counties range from the Black Belt through the northeast corner of the state, including the highly populated Jefferson and Madison Counties.</p>
<p>The National Weather Service (NWS) stations in Birmingham and Huntsville have issued numerous warnings for severe thunderstorms and flash floods in the affected areas.</p>
<p>“Once again, Alabama finds herself facing the threat of severe weather. I urge all Alabamians to closely monitor the weather system as it continues to impact portions of our state, especially if you are in the line of the highest risk storms,” Ivey said in a statement.</p>
<!-- <pre> -->
<!-- </pre> -->
<div id="count_words" style="display: none!important;">

                                            193</div>
<div class="button-wrapper">
<a class="view-more1" href="javascript:void(0)">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>
<span class="count">193 WORDS</span>
</a>
</div>
<div class="dv" style="display: none;"></div>
<div class="button-wrapper" style="display: none;">
<a class="view-more" href="https://yellowhammernews.com/ivey-issues-state-of-emergency-for-28-counties-ahead-of-thursdays-predicted-severe-weather/">
<span><i aria-hidden="true" class="fa fa-angle-down"></i></span>
<span class="keep-reading">Keep reading</span>

<p>“We will continue following this system and stand ready to provide any assistance we are able, should the need arise,” the governor advised.</p>
<p><em>Update 10:55 a.m.:</em></p>
